| 2:37:42| Good afternoon.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9462)|
| 2:37:43| My name is Megan Conley, 1024 Sugar Creek Lane, 37920.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9463)|
| 2:37:48| I'm here to express my concern about our county's possible 287G agreement.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9468)|
| 2:37:53| 287G deputizes local police to act as immigration agents.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9473)|
| 2:37:57| Though this may sound reasonable, independent research has consistently found that 287G is rife with problems,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9477)|
| 2:38:04| including lack of transparency and accountability.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9484)|
| 2:38:08| Three years ago, the Nonpartisan Police Foundation found that immigration enforcement by local police| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9488)|
| 2:38:14| undermines their core public safety mission, diverts scarce resources,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9494)|
| 2:38:20| increases their exposure to liability and litigation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9500)|
| 2:38:24| and exacerbates fear in communities already distrustful of police.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9504)|
| 2:38:29| That same year, our county applied for the full 287G program,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9509)|
| 2:38:34| which includes a task force model and a jail model.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9514)|
| 2:38:37| The jail model, which has been authorized for Knox County,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9517)|
| 2:38:41| will allow designated officers to determine someone's immigration status once they have been arrested,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9521)|
| 2:38:47| regardless of whether the arrest is related to their immigration status.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9527)|
| 2:38:53| The task force model has received a lot of criticism,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9533)|
| 2:38:56| but the jail model is also problematic.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9536)|
| 2:38:59| Not only will it force our county jail to waste time and resources processing immigrants with no criminal record| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9539)|
| 2:39:06| or with only minor infractions, such as traffic violations,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9546)|
| 2:39:10| the jail model may encourage police officers who are not deputized as immigration agents| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9550)|
| 2:39:16| to use the power of arrest to check immigration status.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9556)|
| 2:39:20| The cause for arrest may be something as simple as a traffic violation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9560)|
| 2:39:25| For example, perhaps a driver fails to use a turn signal or has a broken taillight.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9565)|
| 2:39:30| A deputy stops the driver, not because he cares about the traffic violation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9570)|
| 2:39:34| but because he has a hunch that the driver is undocumented.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9574)|
| 2:39:38| This is called a pretextual stop.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9578)|
| 2:39:41| If the deputy thinks the driver is undocumented because she is Latina,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9581)|
| 2:39:45| this is also called racial profiling.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9585)|
| 2:39:48| The driver has a legal ID but does not have a license.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9588)|
| 2:39:51| Instead of issuing a citation for driving without a license,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9591)|
| 2:39:54| which is what often happens in the city of Knoxville,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9594)|
| 2:39:57| the county deputy may take the driver to jail,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9597)|
| 2:40:00| where she will be interrogated about her immigration status.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9600)|
| 2:40:04| For the immigrant stopped with a broken taillight who ends up in deportation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9604)|
| 2:40:08| and the community that hears about this,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9608)|
| 2:40:11| it doesn't matter if this happens through the task force model or the jail model.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9611)|
| 2:40:16| For the crime victim who is now afraid to call the police, it doesn't matter either.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9616)|
| 2:40:21| Any form of 287G offers too much risk and too little reward for our county.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9621)|
| 2:40:27| I would like to pose some questions to Sheriff Jones about these risks.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9627)|
| 2:40:32| How will he properly monitor and train his deputies to prevent and combat| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9632)|
| 2:40:37| the use of racial profiling in pretextual stops?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9637)|
| 2:40:41| How will he ensure that 287G does not undermine trust in the police?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/cocomr267120723?start=9641)|
